If you like specific features of your current desktop client, you can keep using them with your Proton Mail account.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=\"flex flex-col space-y-4 lg:space-y-6\" id=\"section-\u00abr23Re\u00bb\"><div class=\"flex h-full flex-col space-y-2 justify-between text-purple-800\"><div><div class=\"space-y-2\"><div class=\"justify-start\"><h3 class=\"text-xl xl:text-2xl text-purple-800 font-serif\">Work offline when you need to</h3></div><div class=\"space-y-4 text-start\"><div class=\"list-style list-style-type-check list-style-size-7 list-style-color-purple500 list-style-margin-1\"><p>Download your emails using your desktop client when you have a good internet connection, and access them offline later.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></astro-island><astro-island><div class=\"bg-purple-25 text-purple-800\" data-testid=\"content-with-img\"><div class=\"pt-6 lg:pt-12 pb-6 lg:pb-12\"><div class=\"container relative flex flex-col lg:flex-row lg:px-0\"><div class=\"flex w-full flex-col justify-center overflow-hidden lg:w-1/2 xl:pr-24 xl:pl-16 lg:px-12 rounded-2xl lg:order-2\"></div><div class=\"flex w-full flex-col items-start justify-center pb-6 pt-6 text-left lg:w-1/2 lg:pb-0 lg:pt-0 xl:pl-24 xl:pr-16 lg:px-12 lg:order-1\"><div class=\"max-w-135 lg:max-w-150 my-3 lg:px-0\"><h2 class=\"text-3xl lg:text-4xl text-purple-800 font-serif\">Stay protected with Proton Mail\u2019s encryption</h2></div><div class=\"text-purple-800 max-w-135 lg:max-w-150 my-3 space-y-4 text-base lg:mr-20 lg:px-0 lg:text-lg list-style list-style-type-check list-style-size-7 list-style-color-purple500\"><p>Proton Mail Bridge seamlessly encrypts your emails so that only you and your intended recipient can access them. To protect your data, Proton Mail Bridge uses a unique password that is different from your login password and never leaves your computer.</p></div></div></div></div></div></astro-island><div Bridge is a desktop application that runs in the background, encrypting and decrypting messages as they enter and leave your computer. To protect your data, Proton Mail Bridge uses a unique password that is different from your login password and never leaves your computer.Start using Proton Mail BridgeDownload Proton Mail BridgeHow does Proton Mail Bridge work?Proton Mail Bridge is a desktop application that runs in the background, encrypting and decrypting messages as they enter and leave your computer. It lets you add your Proton Mail account to your favorite email client via IMAP/SMTP by creating a local email server on your computer.Is it as secure as Proton Mail\u2019s apps?Proton Mail Bridge was built from the ground up with security in mind to ensure you get a seamless experience with your favorite email client. Your passwords never leave your machine, and we never permanently store your PGP keys or decrypted message data on disc. If you like specific features of your current desktop client, you can keep using them with your Proton Mail account.Work offline when you need toDownload your emails using your desktop client when you have a good internet connection, and access them offline later.Stay protected with Proton Mail\u2019s encryptionProton Mail Bridge seamlessly encrypts your emails so that only you and your intended recipient can access them. To protect your data, Proton Mail Bridge uses a unique password that is different from your login password and never leaves your computer.Start using Proton Mail BridgeDownload Proton Mail BridgeHow does Proton Mail Bridge work?Proton Mail Bridge is a desktop application that runs in the background, encrypting and decrypting messages as they enter and leave your computer. It lets you add your Proton Mail account to your favorite email client via IMAP/SMTP by creating a local email server on your computer.Is it as secure as Proton Mail\u2019s apps?Proton Mail Bridge was built from the ground up with security in mind to ensure you get a seamless experience with your favorite email client. Your passwords never leave your machine, and we never permanently store your PGP keys or decrypted message data on disc. Read this article to learn more about the technical details: How secure is Proton Mail Bridge?Do you have more questions?Head over to our knowledge base",

Proton Mail with your desktop email client\nProton Mail Bridge adds end-to-end encryption to popular email apps, including Outlook, Thunderbird, and Apple Mail. Secure email made easy.\n[System requirements for Proton Mail Bridge](https://proton.me/support/operating-systems-supported-bridge) \nProton Mail Bridge is available only with a paid plan that includes Proton Mail. \n[Upgrade your account](https://proton.me/mail/pricing)\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=e1d75ce6_397e_48aa_a471_60bd21791868_Grid_mobile_54be63f413.png)\n### Keep your habits, stay productive\nYou can use Proton Mail Bridge with popular email clients, such as Microsoft Outlook, Apple Mail, or Mozilla Thunderbird, on all popular operating systems. Keep your existing workflow and store messages locally.\n### Leverage the power of your desktop client\nWe understand you may be particular about your email preferences. If you like specific features of your current desktop client, you can keep using them with your Proton Mail account.\n### Work offline when you need to\nDownload your emails using your desktop client when you have a good internet connection, and access them offline later.\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=70d7ac52_ff6e_4dd2_b171_5f2810b9a604_Section_2_animation_305a4f98a7.png)\n## Stay protected with Proton Mail\u2019s encryption\nProton Mail Bridge seamlessly encrypts your emails so that only you and your intended recipient can access them. To protect your data, Proton Mail Bridge uses a unique password that is different from your login password and never leaves your computer.\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=c&image=image%2Fupload%2Fv1703162849%2Fstatic%2Flogos%2Ficons%2Fbridge_zpnrql.svg)\n## Start using Proton Mail Bridge\n[Download Proton Mail Bridge](https://proton.me/mail/download#bridge)\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=f8193310_a505_445a_9559_f3930c5e5ba2_Bridge_windows_small_shadow_ea64433ca2.png)\n## How does Proton Mail Bridge work?\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=3a42f167_057b_4890_a3b4_f70d67e721ee_Bridge_Cta_2a4e1bab94.png)\nProton Mail Bridge is a desktop application that runs in the background, encrypting and decrypting messages as they enter and leave your computer. It lets you add your Proton Mail account to your favorite email client via IMAP/SMTP by creating a local email server on your computer.\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=4918e2e5_e0f1_4422_b4ad_3d7109c688b8_Application_frame_Apple_V2_33458bd18c.png)\n## Is it as secure as Proton Mail\u2019s apps?\nProton Mail Bridge was built from the ground up with security in mind to ensure you get a seamless experience with your favorite email client. Your passwords never leave your machine, and we never permanently store your PGP keys or decrypted message data on disc. Read this article to learn more about the technical details: [How secure is Proton Mail Bridge?](https://proton.me/blog/bridge-security-model)\n## Do you have more questions?\n[Head over to our Secure email made easy.\nSystem requirements for Proton Mail Bridge\u27e839\u27e9 \nProton Mail Bridge is available only with a paid plan that includes Proton Mail. \nUpgrade your account\u27e810\u27e9\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=e1d75ce6_397e_48aa_a471_60bd21791868_Grid_mobile_54be63f413.png)\n### Keep your habits, stay productive\nYou can use Proton Mail Bridge with popular email clients, such as Microsoft Outlook, Apple Mail, or Mozilla Thunderbird, on all popular operating systems. Keep your existing workflow and store messages locally.\n### Leverage the power of your desktop client\nWe understand you may be particular about your email preferences. If you like specific features of your current desktop client, you can keep using them with your Proton Mail account.\n### Work offline when you need to\nDownload your emails using your desktop client when you have a good internet connection, and access them offline later.\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=70d7ac52_ff6e_4dd2_b171_5f2810b9a604_Section_2_animation_305a4f98a7.png)\n## Stay protected with Proton Mail\u2019s encryption\nProton Mail Bridge seamlessly encrypts your emails so that only you and your intended recipient can access them. To protect your data, Proton Mail Bridge uses a unique password that is different from your login password and never leaves your computer.\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=c&image=image%2Fupload%2Fv1703162849%2Fstatic%2Flogos%2Ficons%2Fbridge_zpnrql.svg)\n## Start using Proton Mail Bridge\nDownload Proton Mail Bridge\u27e840\u27e9\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=f8193310_a505_445a_9559_f3930c5e5ba2_Bridge_windows_small_shadow_ea64433ca2.png)\n## How does Proton Mail Bridge work?\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=3a42f167_057b_4890_a3b4_f70d67e721ee_Bridge_Cta_2a4e1bab94.png)\nProton Mail Bridge is a desktop application that runs in the background, encrypting and decrypting messages as they enter and leave your computer. It lets you add your Proton Mail account to your favorite email client via IMAP/SMTP by creating a local email server on your computer.\n![](https://pmecdn.protonweb.com/image-transformation/?s=s&image=4918e2e5_e0f1_4422_b4ad_3d7109c688b8_Application_frame_Apple_V2_33458bd18c.png)\n## Is it as secure as Proton Mail\u2019s apps?\nProton Mail Bridge was built from the ground up with security in mind to ensure you get a seamless experience with your favorite email client. Your passwords never leave your machine, and we never permanently store your PGP keys or decrypted message data on disc.
